The pressure difference between the higher pressure air below the hull and lower pressure ambient air above it produces lift, which causes the hull to float above the running surface. For stability reasons, the air is typically blown through slots or holes around the outside of a disk- or oval-shaped platform, giving most \r\nhovercraft a characteristic rounded-rectangle shape. Typically this cushion is contained within a flexible \"skirt\", which allows the vehicle to travel over small obstructions without damage.\r\n\r\nEnjoy fast-paced action in our Hovercraft Simulator. For totally addictive and arcade racing, Hovercraft Simulator game is the one.\r\n\r\nHovercraft can be termed as \"ground effect\" or \"water effect\" vehicles. The principal difference is that a hovercraft can lift itself while still, whereas the majority of other designs require forward motion to create lift. These active-motion \"surface effect vehicles\" are known in specific cases as Ekranoplan and Hydrofoils.\r\n\r\nHovercraft Simulator will leave you at the edge of your seat.
